					success : function(data){
				    	callbackCircleFun(data);
				    },
				    error: function(xhr, status, error) {
						alert(error);
					}
				});	
				
			}else {	//상호검색,지역내 검색,반경내 검색 		
				clearFormData();

					if($('#OS_NM').val() != ''){
						//$('#MAP_ZOOM').val(12); //줌 사용시 주석 해제 할것
					} else {
						alert("상호명을 입력 하십시오.");
						$('#OS_NM').focus();
						return;
					}
				}else{
					$('#OS_NM').val("");
				}
				if(validate()) {
					$("#searrgVO").attr({"action":"/searRgSelect.do", "target":"_self"}).submit();
				}
			}
		});

		$('.POLL_DIV_CD').click(function() {
			var poll = document.getElementsByName("POLL_DIV_CD");
			var leng = poll.length;
			var check = 0;
			for(var i=0; i&lt;leng; i++) {
				if(document.getElementsByName("POLL_DIV_CD")[i].checked) {
					check++;
				} else {
					check--;
					break;
				}
			}
			if(check == 6){
				document.getElementById("POLL_DIV_ALL").className = "btn_type2_sel";
				$('#POLL_ALL').val('ALL');
			}else{
				document.getElementById("POLL_DIV_ALL").className = "btn_type2";
				$('#POLL_ALL').val('');
			}
		});

	function fn_excel_download(btn_div) {
		
		$("#BTN_DIV").val(btn_div);
		frm = document.form1;
		frm.action="/download_excel.do";
		frm.target = "_self";
		frm.method = "post";
		frm.submit();
	}
	
	function labelImg(lid){
		$('#'+lid).click();
	}
	
	function checkBrowser() {
		var canUse = false;
		var browserName = "Unknown";
		var browserVer = "";
		var browserVerMain = "";

		if (/MSIE/.test(navigator.userAgent)) {
		  	browserName = "Internet Explorer";
		  	browserVer = /MSIE ([\d\.]+)\;/.exec(navigator.appVersion)[1];
		  	browserVerMain = /(\d+)\./.exec(browserVer)[1];
		 	if(browserVerMain == "8"||browserVerMain == "7"||browserVerMain == "6") {
		   		canUse = true;
		  	}
		}
		return canUse;
	}

		function sigunguGisResult0(data){
			var html = '&lt;option value=""&gt;시/군/구&lt;/option&gt;';
			
			$.each(data, function(idx){
				html += '&lt;option value="'+this.SIGUNGU_NM+'"&gt;'+this.SIGUNGU_NM+'&lt;/option&gt;';
			});
			
			$("#SIGUNGU_NM0").html(html);
		}

		function fn_map0(dong, zoom) {
			
			var mapOpts = {
					center: new olleh.maps.LatLng(37.4852037,127.0344078),
					zoom: zoom,
					disableShadow: true,
					measureControl: false,
					//disableDraggingCursor :false,
					mapTypeId: 'ROADMAP'
				};
					
			map = new olleh.maps.Map(document.getElementById('map_div'), mapOpts);
		}

   				var UNI_ID_VO		= "";
   				var KPETRO_YN 		= "N";
   				var MARKER_ID       = "marker"+'39';
   				var inx 			= '38';

		window.onload = initialize;

		function fn_marker0(inx,markerP, B027_P,D047_P,B034_P,C004_P,K015_P, B027_DT,D047_DT,B034_DT,C004_DT,K015_DT,GIS_X_COOR,GIS_Y_COOR,VLT_YN,SELF_DIV_CD,SEL24_YN,POLL_DIV_CD,OS_NM,DISC_IF_CONTS,SAVE_EVENT_CONTS,REP_EVENT_CONTS,ON_EVENT_CONTS,ETC_BIZ_CONTS,POLL_DIV_NM,PHN_NO,RD_ADDR,CWSH_YN,MAINT_YN,CVS_YN,LPG_YN, UNI_ID, UNI_ID_VO, KPETRO_YN, BIZ_NO, CB_CD, CS_YN) {
			var iconUrl = "/images/user/gis/3-03.png";
			
			//2016.03.21
			if(KPETRO_YN!='Y'){
				if(POLL_DIV_CD == "SOL") iconUrl = "/images/user/gis/3-01.png";			//s-oil 38*37
				else if(POLL_DIV_CD == "E1G") iconUrl = "/images/user/gis/3-02.png";	//e1 38*37
				else if(POLL_DIV_CD == "SKE") iconUrl = "/images/user/gis/3-03.png";		//sk 31*31
				else if(POLL_DIV_CD == "SKG") iconUrl = "/images/user/gis/3-15.png";	//skg 38*37
				else if(POLL_DIV_CD == "HDO") iconUrl = "/images/user/gis/3-07.png";	//hd 38*37
				else if(POLL_DIV_CD == "GSC") iconUrl = "/images/user/gis/3-08.png";	//gs 38*37
				else if(POLL_DIV_CD == "ETC") iconUrl = "/images/user/gis/3-09.png";	//etc 38*37
				else if(POLL_DIV_CD == "NCO") iconUrl = "/images/user/gis/3-09.png";	//etc 38*37
				else if(POLL_DIV_CD == "RTO" || POLL_DIV_CD == "RTX") iconUrl = "/images/user/gis/3-12.png";		//rto 31*31	
				else if(POLL_DIV_CD == "NHO") iconUrl = "/images/user/gis/3-12.png";
				//alert("OS_NM:"+OS_NM+"POLL_DIV_CD:"+POLL_DIV_CD + ",iconUrl:" + iconUrl);
			}else{
				if(POLL_DIV_CD == "SOL") iconUrl = "/images/user/gis/marker_kp_soil_2.png";			//s-oil 38*37
				else if(POLL_DIV_CD == "E1G") iconUrl = "/images/user/gis/3-02.png";	//e1 38*37
				else if(POLL_DIV_CD == "SKE") iconUrl = "/images/user/gis/marker_kp_sk_2.png";		//sk 31*31
				else if(POLL_DIV_CD == "SKG") iconUrl = "/images/user/gis/3-15.png";	//skg 38*37
				else if(POLL_DIV_CD == "HDO") iconUrl = "/images/user/gis/marker_kp_hd_2.png";	//hd 38*37
				else if(POLL_DIV_CD == "GSC") iconUrl = "/images/user/gis/marker_kp_gs_2.png";	//gs 38*37
				else if(POLL_DIV_CD == "ETC") iconUrl = "/images/user/gis/marker_kp_pb_2.png";	//etc 38*37
				else if(POLL_DIV_CD == "NCO") iconUrl = "/images/user/gis/marker_kp_pb_2.png";	//etc 38*37
				else if(POLL_DIV_CD == "RTO" || POLL_DIV_CD == "RTX") iconUrl = "/images/user/gis/marker_kp_rto_2.png";		//rto 31*31	
				else if(POLL_DIV_CD == "NHO") iconUrl = "/images/user/gis/marker_kp_rto_2.png";
				//alert("OS_NM:"+OS_NM+"POLL_DIV_CD:"+POLL_DIV_CD + ",iconUrl:" + iconUrl);
			}
			
			var markerP = new olleh.maps.overlay.Marker({
			  position: new olleh.maps.Katech(GIS_X_COOR, GIS_Y_COOR),
			  icon: {
				 url: iconUrl,    // 아이콘 url만 변경
				 /* size: new olleh.maps.Size(43, 45)	 */
			      size: new olleh.maps.Size(38, 37) 
			  },
			  map: map
			});
			
			if(UNI_ID == UNI_ID_VO){
				fn_osPop(markerP, B034_P,B027_P,D047_P,C004_P,K015_P, B034_DT,B027_DT,D047_DT,C004_DT,K015_DT,GIS_X_COOR,GIS_Y_COOR,DISC_IF_CONTS,SAVE_EVENT_CONTS,REP_EVENT_CONTS,ON_EVENT_CONTS,ETC_BIZ_CONTS,VLT_YN,SELF_DIV_CD,SEL24_YN,POLL_DIV_CD,OS_NM,POLL_DIV_NM,PHN_NO,RD_ADDR,CWSH_YN,MAINT_YN,CVS_YN,LPG_YN,KPETRO_YN,UNI_ID,BIZ_NO, CB_CD, CS_YN);
			}
			
			markerP.onEvent('click',function (event, payload) {
				if(osinfo != null)	osinfo.close();
				if(vltinfo != null)	vltinfo.close();
				
				if(VLT_YN != 'Y'){ //불법행위업소 아니면
					fn_osPop(markerP, B034_P,B027_P,D047_P,C004_P,K015_P, B034_DT,B027_DT,D047_DT,C004_DT,K015_DT,GIS_X_COOR,GIS_Y_COOR,DISC_IF_CONTS,SAVE_EVENT_CONTS,REP_EVENT_CONTS,ON_EVENT_CONTS,ETC_BIZ_CONTS,VLT_YN,SELF_DIV_CD,SEL24_YN,POLL_DIV_CD,OS_NM,POLL_DIV_NM,PHN_NO,RD_ADDR,CWSH_YN,MAINT_YN,CVS_YN,LPG_YN,KPETRO_YN,UNI_ID,BIZ_NO, CB_CD,CS_YN);
				}else{
					//불법행위업소면 불법행위관련정보를 가져와서 infowindow를 띄운다.
					//20170907
					if(UNI_ID != null &amp;&amp; UNI_ID != ""){
						fnVolatInfowindow(UNI_ID, LPG_YN, markerP);	
					}
				}
			});
			
			markerP.onEvent('mouseover',function (event) {
				$('.ollehmap-event').attr('title',OS_NM);
				fn_tooltip(markerP, GIS_X_COOR, GIS_Y_COOR, VLT_YN, SELF_DIV_CD, SEL24_YN, B027_P, D047_P, LPG_YN, K015_P, KPETRO_YN);
			});
			
			markerP.onEvent('mouseout',function (event) {
				tooltipinfo.close();
			});
			
			OsMarker[inx] = markerP;
			//clusterer.add(markerP);
			//clusterer.setMap(map);
			var OsMarkerJsonData = {
					"marker" : markerP,
					"GIS_X_COOR" : GIS_X_COOR,
					"GIS_Y_COOR" : GIS_Y_COOR,
					"VLT_YN" : VLT_YN,
					"SELF_DIV_CD" : SELF_DIV_CD,
					"B027_P" : B027_P,
					"D047_P" : D047_P,
					"LPG_YN" : LPG_YN,
					"K015_P" : K015_P,
					"type"   : "rg"
			};
			OsMarkerJsonArr.push(OsMarkerJsonData);
		}
		

		
		function preLiteDelete(){
			for (var i = 0; i &lt; OsMarker.length; i++) {
				OsMarker[i].setVisible(false);
			}
		}
		
		//이전 데이터 삭제
		function preDataDelete() {
			for (var i = 0; i &lt; OsMarker.length; i++) {
				OsMarker[i].setVisible(false);
			}
			$('#head11').empty();
			$('#head11_1').empty();	//20170816 ysj 휘발유탭 경유 가격 초기화 추가
			$('#body11').empty();
			$('#head22').empty();
			$('#body22').empty();
			$('#head33').empty();
			$('#head33_1').empty(); //20170816 ysj 경유탭 경유 가격 초기화	추가
			$('#body33').empty();
			$('#head44').empty();
			$('#body44').empty();
			$('#totCnt1').text(0);
		}
		
		function geocode_center0(data){
			var geocoderResult = geocoder.parseGeocode(data);
			if(geocoderResult["errcd"] != "0") {
				osChoicePos = new olleh.maps.LatLng(35.5644654, 129.3084977);	//울산석유공사
			}else {
/* 				if($('#MAP_FIRST_X').val() != "" &amp;&amp; $('#MAP_FIRST_Y').val() != ""){
					osChoicePos = new olleh.maps.Katech($('#MAP_FIRST_X').val(), $('#MAP_FIRST_Y').val());
				}else {
					if(Number(geocoderResult["count"]) &gt; 0){
						var infoArr = geocoderResult["infoarr"];
						osChoicePos = new olleh.maps.UTMK(infoArr[0].x, infoArr[0].y);
					}else {
						osChoicePos = new olleh.maps.LatLng(35.5644654, 129.3084977);	//울산석유공사
					}
				} */ 
				if(Number(geocoderResult["count"]) &gt; 0){
					if($('#MAP_FIRST_X').val() != "" &amp;&amp; $('#MAP_FIRST_Y').val() != "") {	
					
						osChoicePos = new olleh.maps.Katech($('#MAP_FIRST_X').val(), $('#MAP_FIRST_Y').val());
					}else {					
						var infoArr = geocoderResult["infoarr"];
						osChoicePos = new olleh.maps.UTMK(infoArr[0].x, infoArr[0].y);
					}
				}else {
					//osChoicePos = new olleh.maps.LatLng(35.5644654, 129.3084977);	//울산석유공사
				}				
			}
			map.setCenter(osChoicePos);
		}
		
		function geocode_center_nm(data){
			var geocoderResult = geocoder.parseGeocode(data);
			if(geocoderResult["errcd"] != "0") {
				//osChoicePos = new olleh.maps.LatLng(35.5644654, 129.3084977);	//울산석유공사
			}else {
				if(Number(geocoderResult["count"]) &gt; 0){
					if($('#MAP_FIRST_X').val() != "" &amp;&amp; $('#MAP_FIRST_Y').val() != "") {	
						osChoicePos = new olleh.maps.Katech($('#MAP_FIRST_X').val(), $('#MAP_FIRST_Y').val());
					}else {					
						var infoArr = geocoderResult["infoarr"];
						osChoicePos = new olleh.maps.UTMK(infoArr[0].x, infoArr[0].y);
					}
					
					map.setCenter(osChoicePos);
					
				}else {
	   	   				var sido_nm = "서울특별시";
   	   	   				var sigungu_nm = "서초구";
   	   	   				var sigungu_nm_arr = sigungu_nm.split("시");
   	   	   				if(sigungu_nm_arr != null &amp;&amp; sigungu_nm_arr != undefined &amp;&amp; sigungu_nm_arr.length &gt; 1){
   	   	   					if(sigungu_nm_arr.length &gt; 3){
	   	   	   					sigungu_nm = sigungu_nm_arr[0] + "시 "+sigungu_nm_arr[1]  +" "+ sigungu_nm_arr[2]; 	
   	   	   					}else{
	   	   	   					sigungu_nm = sigungu_nm_arr[0] +"시 "+ sigungu_nm_arr[1];
   	   	   					}
   	   	   				}
   	   	   				var addrS = "";
   	   	   				var dong_nm = "";
/*    	   	   				if("" != ""){
   	   	   					dong_nm = "";
   	   	   				} */
   	   	   				addrS = sido_nm +" "+ sigungu_nm ; 
   	   	   				geocoder = new olleh.maps.Geocoder("YjlmODYzMDE4N2ViNGU3OGEzMDE0MWRjZDcwNTdiZmI6NzViMmU2ZjFkYjVmYmMxY2Q1MWVlNjJhYjY0NDhkMWY="); 
   	   	   				geocoder.geocode({
   	   	   					type:0,
   	   						addr:addrS,
   	   						addrcdtype:1
   	   	   				},
   	   	   				"geocode_center_nm2"
   	   	   				);
				}				
			}
			
		}	
		
		function geocode_center_nm2(data){
			var geocoderResult = geocoder.parseGeocode(data);
			if(geocoderResult["errcd"] != "0") {
				//osChoicePos = new olleh.maps.LatLng(35.5644654, 129.3084977);	//울산석유공사
			}else {
				if(Number(geocoderResult["count"]) &gt; 0){
					if($('#MAP_FIRST_X').val() != "" &amp;&amp; $('#MAP_FIRST_Y').val() != "") {	
						osChoicePos = new olleh.maps.Katech($('#MAP_FIRST_X').val(), $('#MAP_FIRST_Y').val());
					}else {					
						var infoArr = geocoderResult["infoarr"];
						osChoicePos = new olleh.maps.UTMK(infoArr[0].x, infoArr[0].y);
					}
					
					map.setCenter(osChoicePos);
					
				}		
			}
			
		}	
		
		function geocode_center_map(data){
			var osChoicePos_map = new olleh.maps.UTMK($('#MAP_CENTER_X').val(), $('#MAP_CENTER_Y').val());
			//alert("geocode_center_map:"+osChoicePos_map);
			map.setCenter(osChoicePos_map);
		}
		
		function geocode_center_main(data){
			var osChoicePos_main = new olleh.maps.UTMK(osinfo.getPosition().x, osinfo.getPosition().y+2000);
			//alert("geocode_center_map:"+osChoicePos_map);
			map.setCenter(osChoicePos_main);
		}

		function poiSearchName1(data) {
			var resultStr = data.ktAPIData;
			var html = '';
			if(resultStr != null &amp;&amp; resultStr != "" &amp;&amp; resultStr.length &lt;= 0) {
				html +=	'&lt;div class="desc_box"&gt;'+
				'	&lt;div class="d_left"&gt;'+
				'		&lt;span class="search_result"&gt;검색결과 (총 &lt;span class="tc_spot"&gt;15&lt;/span&gt;개)&lt;/span&gt;'+
				'	&lt;/div&gt;'+
				'&lt;/div&gt;'+
				'&lt;div class="t_center overflow_gis mgb_7" style="height:396px;" &gt;'+
				'&lt;table class="tbl_type10" summary="주유소이름, 주소 등을 확인 할 수 있습니다"&gt;'+
				'&lt;caption&gt;주유소목록검색 결과&lt;/caption&gt;'+
				'&lt;colgroup&gt;'+
				'		&lt;col style="width: 110px;"&gt;'+
				'		&lt;col&gt;'+
				'		&lt;col style="width: 85px;"&gt;'+
				'&lt;/colgroup&gt;'+				
				'&lt;thead&gt;'+
				'	&lt;tr&gt;'+
				'		&lt;th scope="row" class="t_center" colspan="3"&gt;선택목록&lt;/th&gt;'+
				'	&lt;/tr&gt;'+
				'&lt;/thead&gt;'+				
				'&lt;tbody&gt;'+
				'	&lt;tr&gt;'+
				'		&lt;td class="rlist t_center" colspan="3"&gt;'+
				'			검색결과가 없습니다'+
				'		&lt;/td&gt;'+
				'	&lt;/tr&gt;'+
				'&lt;/tbody&gt;'+
				'&lt;/table&gt;'+
				'&lt;/div&gt;';					
			} else {
				html +=	'&lt;div class="desc_box"&gt;'+
				'	&lt;div class="d_left"&gt;'+
				'		&lt;span class="search_result"&gt;검색결과 (총 &lt;span class="tc_spot"&gt;'+resultStr.length+'&lt;/span&gt;개)&lt;/span&gt;'+
				'	&lt;/div&gt;'+
				'&lt;/div&gt;'+
				'&lt;div class="t_center overflow_gis mgb_7" style="height:396px;" &gt;'+
				'&lt;table class="tbl_type10" summary="주유소이름, 주소 등을 확인 할 수 있습니다"&gt;'+
				'&lt;caption&gt;주유소목록검색 결과&lt;/caption&gt;'+
				'&lt;colgroup&gt;'+
				'		&lt;col style="width: 110px;"&gt;'+
				'		&lt;col&gt;'+
				'		&lt;col style="width: 85px;"&gt;'+
				'&lt;/colgroup&gt;'+				
				'&lt;thead&gt;'+
				'	&lt;tr&gt;'+
				'		&lt;th scope="row" class="t_center" colspan="3"&gt;선택목록&lt;/th&gt;'+
				'	&lt;/tr&gt;'+
				'&lt;/thead&gt;'+				
				'&lt;tbody&gt;';
				for(var i=0; i&lt;resultStr.length; i++) {
					html +=	'	&lt;tr&gt;'+
					'		&lt;td class="rlist"&gt;'+
					'			&lt;a  href="javascript:fn_start('+resultStr[i].X+','+resultStr[i].Y+');"&gt;'+resultStr[i].NAME+'&lt;/a&gt;'+
					'		&lt;/td&gt;'+
					'		&lt;td class="tc_333 t_left"&gt;'+resultStr[i].SIDO+" "+resultStr[i].SGG+" "+resultStr[i].DONG+'&lt;/td&gt;'+
					'		&lt;td&gt;'+
					'			&lt;a class="btn_type2_tbl" href="javascript:fn_start('+resultStr[i].X+','+resultStr[i].Y+');" title="선택"&gt;&lt;span&gt;선택&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/a&gt;'+
					'		&lt;/td&gt;'+
					'	&lt;/tr&gt;';
				}	
				html +=	'&lt;/tbody&gt;'+
				'&lt;/table&gt;'+
				'&lt;/div&gt;';				
			}
			$('#templ_list').html(html);
		}

		function fn_start(x, y) {
			$('#templ_list1').show();   
			$('#POI_SEARCH').hide();
			$('#RACT_SEARCH').hide();
			$('#templ_list').hide();
	        map.onEvent('dragend',function (event, payload) {
				if(GetSearchBound()){
					//commonFormAjax('/searRgPlaceAjax.d', 'searrgVO', callbackPlaceFun);
					$.ajax({
						type  : "POST",
						url   : "/searRgPlaceAjax.do",
						data  : $("#searrgVO").serialize(),
						dataType : "json",
						//contentType: "application/json; charset=utf-8", 
						success : function(data){
					    	callbackPlaceFun(data);
					    },
					    error: function(xhr, status, error) {
							alert(error);
						}
					});	
				}
	        });
	        
			fn_start_marker0(x, y, "N"); //선택지역에 아이콘 표시
		}
		
		//출발지 아이콘
		function fn_start_marker0(GIS_X_COOR,GIS_Y_COOR,real) {
			if(real == "N")	{
				startMarker = new olleh.maps.overlay.Marker({
					position: new olleh.maps.UTMK(GIS_X_COOR, GIS_Y_COOR),
					map: map
				});
			}
			else {
				var iconUrl = "/images/user/gis/g1.png";
				startMarker = new olleh.maps.overlay.Marker({
					position: new olleh.maps.UTMK(GIS_X_COOR, GIS_Y_COOR),
					icon: {
						url: iconUrl,    // 아이콘 url만 변경
						size: new olleh.maps.Size(39, 41)				
					},
					map: map
				});
			}
			map.setCenter(new olleh.maps.UTMK(GIS_X_COOR, GIS_Y_COOR));
			//ajax로 지도영역내의 주유소를 검색하여 마커를 생성한다.
			//commonAjax("/searRgPlaceAjax.d", "RD_DIV_NM="+RD_DIV_NM+"&amp;SANGHA_DIV_NM="+SANGHA_DIV_NM, callbackPlaceFun);
			//clearFormData();
			map.setZoom(11);
			setTimeout(function(){ 
				if(GetSearchBound()){
					//commonFormAjax('/searRgPlaceAjax.d', 'searrgVO', callbackPlaceFun);
					$.ajax({
						type  : "POST",
						url   : "/searRgPlaceAjax.do",
						data  : $("#searrgVO").serialize(),
						dataType : "json",
						//contentType: "application/json; charset=utf-8", 
						success : function(data){
					    	callbackPlaceFun(data);
					    },
					    error: function(xhr, status, error) {
							alert(error);
						}
					});	
				}
			}, 500);
		}

		function callbackPlaceFun(data){
			
			//map.setZoom(11);
			
			var resultJsonList = data.list;
			var resultJsonList2 = data.list2;

		//팝업 리스너
		function popLis(){
			$('a[name="pop"]').click(function(){
				var pops;
				//20170816 ysj 비교 조건 추가
				if($('#os_layer11').attr('class') == 'sel'){	//고급 휘발유
					pops = pop2;
				} else if($('#os_layer22').attr('class') == 'sel'){ //휘발유
					pops = pop;
				}else if($('#os_layer33').attr('class') == 'sel'){ //경유
					pops = pop3;
				}else if($('#os_layer44').attr('class') == 'sel'){ //등유
					pops = pop4;
				}else{
					pops = pop;
				}
				var dname = parseInt($(this).attr('data-name'));
				var i = dname;
					fn_osPop(OsMarker[i], pops[i].B034_P, pops[i].B027_P, pops[i].D047_P, pops[i].C004_P, pops[i].K015_P, pops[i].B034_DT, pops[i].B027_DT, pops[i].D047_DT, pops[i].C004_DT, pops[i].K015_DT, pops[i].GIS_X_COOR, pops[i].GIS_Y_COOR, pops[i].DISC_IF_CONTS, pops[i].SAVE_EVENT_CONTS, pops[i].REP_EVENT_CONTS,pops[i].ON_EVENT_CONTS, pops[i].ETC_BIZ_CONTS, pops[i].VLT_YN, pops[i].SELF_DIV_CD, pops[i].SEL24_YN, pops[i].POLL_DIV_CD, pops[i].OS_NM, pops[i].POLL_DIV_NM, pops[i].PHN_NO, pops[i].RD_ADDR, pops[i].CWSH_YN, pops[i].MAINT_YN, pops[i].CVS_YN, pops[i].LPG_YN, pops[i].KPETRO_YN,pops[i].UNI_ID, pops[i].BIZ_NO,  pops[i].CB_CD, pops[i].CS_YN);	
			});
		}
		
		function validate() {
			var frm = document.form1;        
	       
		    var obj = frm.SIDO_NM0;
			var val = obj.selectedIndex;
			if(val &lt; 1){
				alert("시도를 선택하여주세요");
				return false;
			}
		    var obj = frm.SIGUNGU_NM0;
			var val = obj.selectedIndex;
			if(val &lt; 1){
				alert("시군구를 선택하여주세요");
				return false;
			}
			return true;
		}
		
		function validate2() {
			if($('#GIS_X_COOR_S').val() == "") { alert("범위설정이 되지 않았습니다. 재설정하세요."); return false; }
			if($('#GIS_Y_COOR_E').val() == "") { alert("범위설정이 되지 않았습니다. 재설정하세요."); return false; }
			if($('#GIS_X_COOR_E').val() == "") { alert("범위설정이 되지 않았습니다. 재설정하세요."); return false; }
			if($('#GIS_Y_COOR_S').val() == "") { alert("범위설정이 되지 않았습니다. 재설정하세요."); return false; }
			return true;
		}
		
		function GetSearchBound() {

			if (map == null) return false;
// 			console.log("map.getZoom()========================="+ map.getZoom());
			if ( map.getZoom() &lt; 5 ) {
			//	map.setZoom(7);
				alert( "확대된 지도 레벨에서 검색이 가능합니다.\r\n우측 지도 레벨바를 6레벨 이상으로 설정해 주십시요!" );

				return false;
			}
			

			var latlngBound = map.getBounds();
			var min = latlngBound.getLeftTopCoord();
			var max = latlngBound.getRightBottomCoord();
			var aftCoord_max = olleh.maps.Katech.valueOf(max);
			var aftCoord_min = olleh.maps.Katech.valueOf(min);
			//console.log(aftCoord_max.x+" : "+aftCoord_max.y);
			//console.log(aftCoord_min.x+" : "+aftCoord_min.y);
			$('#GIS_X_COOR_S').val(aftCoord_min.x);
			$('#GIS_X_COOR_E').val(aftCoord_max.x);
			$('#GIS_Y_COOR_E').val(aftCoord_min.y);
			$('#GIS_Y_COOR_S').val(aftCoord_max.y);
			return true;
		}
		
		
		function GetCircleSearchBound() {
			if (map == null) return;
			if ( map.getZoom() &lt; 8 ) {
				alert( "확대된 지도 레벨에서 검색이 가능합니다.\r\n우측 레벨바를 8레벨 이상으로 설정해 주십시요!" );
				return null;
			}
			if (circle == null) return;

			var latlngBound = circle.getBounds();
			var min = latlngBound.getLeftTopCoord();
			var max = latlngBound.getRightBottomCoord();
			var aftCoord_max = olleh.maps.Katech.valueOf(max);
			var aftCoord_min = olleh.maps.Katech.valueOf(min);

			$('#GIS_X_COOR_S').val(aftCoord_min.x);
			$('#GIS_X_COOR_E').val(aftCoord_max.x);
			$('#GIS_Y_COOR_E').val(aftCoord_min.y);
			$('#GIS_Y_COOR_S').val(aftCoord_max.y);
		}
		

	    var startPoint;
	    var endPoint;
		var circleDiv;
		var Radius_IsDrawing = false;
		
	    function SetCircleOnMap() {    
		       
	    	if (map == null) return;
	    	
	        alert("지도에서 마우스 드레그로 반경을 설정해 주세요.");
	        
	        if (circle) {
	        	circle.setMap(null);
	            circle = null;
	    		startPoint = null;
	    		endPoint = null;	   
	    		
	    	    endPointMarker.setVisible(false);
		    	   
	        	circleLine.setVisible(false);	    		
	        }
	        
	        
	        map.draggable = false;
	        
 	        var elem = document.getElementById('map_div');
	        
  	        olleh.maps.util.dom.setStyle(elem, "cursor", "crosshair");
	        olleh.maps.util.dom.setStyle(elem, "opacity", "0.5");
	        olleh.maps.util.dom.setStyle(elem, "backgroundColor", "black");   
             
             map.onEvent('dragstart',function (event) {
            	map.draggable = false;
             	startPoint = event.getCoord();
            	Radius_IsDrawing = true;
            	event.preventDefault();
            });	 
             
             map.onEvent('drag',function (event) {
 	        	map.draggable = false;
	        	endPoint = event.getCoord();
	        	var pos  = event.getCoord();
	        	if(map.isValidCoord(pos) &amp;&amp; Radius_IsDrawing == true){
	        		
		            drawCircle(startPoint, endPoint, pos);
		            //map.unsubscribeEvent('mouseup', '', '');
	        	}	
	        	event.preventDefault();
            });	   
             
             map.onEvent('dragend',function (event) {
 	        	var pos = event.getCoord();

	        	if(map.isValidCoord(pos)){
		        	endPoint = event.getCoord();
		            drawCircle(startPoint, endPoint, pos);
		            
			        var elem = document.getElementById('map_div');
		            olleh.maps.util.dom.setStyle(elem, "cursor", "default");
		            olleh.maps.util.dom.setStyle(elem, "opacity", "");
		            olleh.maps.util.dom.setStyle(elem, "background", "");    
	        	}	
	            map.unsubscribeEvent('dragstart', '', '');
	            map.unsubscribeEvent('drag', '', '');
	            map.unsubscribeEvent('dragend', '', '');
	        	event.preventDefault();
	        	Radius_IsDrawing = false;
	        	$('a[data-id="closeC"]').unbind('click');
		        $('a[data-id="closeC"]').click(function(){
		        	if(circle!=null) circle.setVisible(false);
					if(circleLine!=null) circleLine.setVisible(false);
					if(endPointMarker!=null) endPointMarker.setVisible(false);
				});
            });	
            
	    }
	    
	    var circle; 
	    var circleLine ;
	    var path ;
	    var circleText;
	    var markerOptions;
	    var endPointMarker;
	    function drawCircle(startPoint, endPoint, pos) {
	
	        Radius_Distance = Math.sqrt(Math.pow(endPoint.x - startPoint.x, 2) + Math.pow(endPoint.y - startPoint.y, 2));//startPoint.distanceFrom(endPoint); // meters
	        if (circle) {
	        	circle.setMap(null);
	            circle = null;
	        }
	    	
	     	circle = new olleh.maps.vector.Circle({
	            map: map,
	            center: new olleh.maps.UTMK(startPoint),
	            draggable : false,
	            radius: Radius_Distance,
	            strokeColor: "#0000ff",
	     	    strokeOpacity: 0.8,
	     	    strokeWeight: 2,            
	            fillColor: "#0000ff",
	            fillOpacity: 0.1
	          });
	     	
	   
	        if (circleLine) {
	        	circleLine.setMap(null);
	        	circleLine = null;
	        	//circleLine.erase();
	        } 
			path = new olleh.maps.Path([
			           	             new olleh.maps.UTMK(startPoint),
			           	             new olleh.maps.UTMK(endPoint)
			           	        ]);

	        circleLine = new olleh.maps.vector.Polyline({
		         map: map,
		         path: path,
	    		strokeColor: "blue",
	    		strokeOpacity: 0.7,
	    		strokeWeight: 2
	        });

	        //test start
	       if (endPointMarker) {
	    	   endPointMarker.setMap(null);
	    	   endPointMarker = null;
	        	//circleLine.erase();
	        } 
	        
	       var miter = startPoint.distanceTo(endPoint);
	       var distInfo = "";
	       if (miter) {
	            distInfo = (miter &gt; 1000) ? (Math.round(miter / 10) / 100 + "km") : (Math.round(miter) + "m");
	        }
	       var markerCaption = {
					title : "반경 : "+distInfo+"  &lt;a data-id='closeC'&gt;X&lt;/a&gt;",
					background : false,
					backgroundColor: "white",
					backgroundBorder: false,
					fontColor : "red",
					fontFace : "굴림체",
					position: "TOP", //"BOTTOM"
					minZoom: 1,
					maxZoom : 10
			};
	        
	        var iconUrl = "/images/user/gis/g1.png";
			endPointMarker = new olleh.maps.overlay.Marker({
				position: new olleh.maps.UTMK(endPoint),
				icon: {
					url: iconUrl,    // 아이콘 url만 변경
					size: new olleh.maps.Size(0, 0)				
				},
				caption : markerCaption,
				map: map
			});			
	        //test end
	    }		
	    
	    function ClearRadius(){
	    	alert("ClearRadius");
	    }
		
</script>
</head>
